import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cpp_source = """
void fused_transformer_launch(
    torch::Tensor x,
    torch::Tensor output,
    torch::Tensor norm1_weight,
    torch::Tensor norm1_bias,
    torch::Tensor qkv_weight,
    torch::Tensor qkv_bias,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_weight,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_bias,
    torch::Tensor norm2_weight,
    torch::Tensor norm2_bias,
    torch::Tensor fc1_weight,
    torch::Tensor fc1_bias,
    torch::Tensor fc2_weight,
    torch::Tensor fc2_bias,
    torch::Tensor fc_out_weight,
    torch::Tensor fc_out_bias,
    int num_layers,
    int num_heads
);
"""

cuda_code = r"""
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>

__global__ void fused_transformer_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    float* __restrict__ output,
    const float* __restrict__ norm1_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ norm1_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ qkv_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ qkv_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ out_proj_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ out_proj_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ norm2_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ norm2_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ fc1_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ fc1_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ fc2_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ fc2_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ fc_out_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ fc_out_bias,
    int B, int num_layers, int seq_len, int embed_dim, int num_heads, int mlp_dim, int num_classes
) {
    int b = blockIdx.x;
    if (b >= B) return;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    int head_dim = embed_dim / num_heads;
    float scale = rsqrtf((float)head_dim);
    
    extern __shared__ float s[];
    float* s_x = s;
    float* s_buf = s_x + seq_len * embed_dim;
    float* s_t1 = s_buf + seq_len * embed_dim;
    float* s_t2 = s_t1 + seq_len * 3 * embed_dim;
    
    const float* x_g = x + b * seq_len * embed_dim;
    for (int i = tid; i < seq_len * embed_dim; i += blockDim.x) {
        s_x[i] = x_g[i];
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    for (int layer = 0; layer < num_layers; layer++) {
        // Self-attention block: compute QKV from s_x
        const float* w_qkv = qkv_weight + layer * embed_dim * 3 * embed_dim;
        const float* b_qkv = qkv_bias + layer * 3 * embed_dim;
        int qkv_size = seq_len * 3 * embed_dim;
        for (int out_idx = tid; out_idx < qkv_size; out_idx += blockDim.x) {
            int token = out_idx / (3 * embed_dim);
            int dim = out_idx % (3 * embed_dim);
            float acc = b_qkv[dim];
            for (int i = 0; i < embed_dim; i++) {
                acc += s_x[token * embed_dim + i] * w_qkv[i * 3 * embed_dim + dim];
            }
            s_t1[out_idx] = acc;
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // Attention scores
        int score_size = num_heads * seq_len * seq_len;
        for (int idx = tid; idx < score_size; idx += blockDim.x) {
            int head = idx / (seq_len * seq_len);
            int q_tok = (idx % (seq_len * seq_len)) / seq_len;
            int k_tok = idx % seq_len;
            float acc = 0.0f;
            for (int d = 0; d < head_dim; d++) {
                float q = s_t1[q_tok * 3 * embed_dim + head * head_dim + d];
                float k = s_t1[k_tok * 3 * embed_dim + embed_dim + head * head_dim + d];
                acc += q * k;
            }
            s_t2[idx] = acc * scale;
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // Softmax
        for (int idx = tid; idx < num_heads * seq_len; idx += blockDim.x) {
            int head = idx / seq_len;
            int q_tok = idx % seq_len;
            int base = head * seq_len * seq_len + q_tok * seq_len;
            float maxv = s_t2[base];
            for (int k = 1; k < seq_len; k++) maxv = fmaxf(maxv, s_t2[base + k]);
            float sum = 0.0f;
            for (int k = 0; k < seq_len; k++) {
                s_t2[base + k] = expf(s_t2[base + k] - maxv);
                sum += s_t2[base + k];
            }
            for (int k = 0; k < seq_len; k++) s_t2[base + k] *= (1.0f / sum);
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // Attention output
        for (int idx = tid; idx < seq_len * embed_dim; idx += blockDim.x) {
            int token = idx / embed_dim;
            int dim = idx % embed_dim;
            int head = dim / head_dim;
            int hd = dim % head_dim;
            float acc = 0.0f;
            for (int k = 0; k < seq_len; k++) {
                float score = s_t2[head * seq_len * seq_len + token * seq_len + k];
                float v = s_t1[k * 3 * embed_dim + 2 * embed_dim + head * head_dim + hd];
                acc += score * v;
            }
            s_t1[idx] = acc;
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // Out proj
        const float* w_op = out_proj_weight + layer * embed_dim * embed_dim;
        const float* b_op = out_proj_bias + layer * embed_dim;
        for (int out_idx = tid; out_idx < seq_len * embed_dim; out_idx += blockDim.x) {
            int token = out_idx / embed_dim;
            int dim = out_idx % embed_dim;
            float acc = b_op[dim];
            for (int i = 0; i < embed_dim; i++) {
                acc += s_t1[token * embed_dim + i] * w_op[i * embed_dim + dim];
            }
            s_t2[out_idx] = acc;
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // Residual + LayerNorm (post-LN)
        if (tid == 0) {
            for (int t = 0; t < seq_len; t++) {
                float mean = 0.0f;
                for (int j = 0; j < embed_dim; j++) mean += (s_x[t * embed_dim + j] + s_t2[t * embed_dim + j]);
                mean *= (1.0f / (float)embed_dim);
                float var = 0.0f;
                for (int j = 0; j < embed_dim; j++) {
                    float d = (s_x[t * embed_dim + j] + s_t2[t * embed_dim + j]) - mean;
                    var += d * d;
                }
                var *= (1.0f / (float)embed_dim);
                float inv_std = rsqrtf(var + 1e-5f);
                const float* n1w = norm1_weight + layer * embed_dim;
                const float* n1b = norm1_bias + layer * embed_dim;
                for (int j = 0; j < embed_dim; j++) {
                    s_x[t * embed_dim + j] = ((s_x[t * embed_dim + j] + s_t2[t * embed_dim + j]) - mean) * inv_std * n1w[j] + n1b[j];
                }
            }
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // FFN: linear1
        const float* w_fc1 = fc1_weight + layer * embed_dim * mlp_dim;
        const float* b_fc1 = fc1_bias + layer * mlp_dim;
        for (int out_idx = tid; out_idx < seq_len * mlp_dim; out_idx += blockDim.x) {
            int token = out_idx / mlp_dim;
            int dim = out_idx % mlp_dim;
            float acc = b_fc1[dim];
            for (int i = 0; i < embed_dim; i++) {
                acc += s_x[token * embed_dim + i] * w_fc1[i * mlp_dim + dim];
            }
            s_t2[out_idx] = fmaxf(acc, 0.0f);
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // FFN: linear2
        const float* w_fc2 = fc2_weight + layer * mlp_dim * embed_dim;
        const float* b_fc2 = fc2_bias + layer * embed_dim;
        for (int out_idx = tid; out_idx < seq_len * embed_dim; out_idx += blockDim.x) {
            int token = out_idx / embed_dim;
            int dim = out_idx % embed_dim;
            float acc = b_fc2[dim];
            for (int i = 0; i < mlp_dim; i++) {
                acc += s_t2[token * mlp_dim + i] * w_fc2[i * embed_dim + dim];
            }
            s_t1[out_idx] = acc;
        }
        __syncthreads();
        
        // Residual + LayerNorm (post-LN)
        if (tid == 0) {
            for (int t = 0; t < seq_len; t++) {
                float mean = 0.0f;
                for (int j = 0; j < embed_dim; j++) mean += (s_x[t * embed_dim + j] + s_t1[t * embed_dim + j]);
                mean *= (1.0f / (float)embed_dim);
                float var = 0.0f;
                for (int j = 0; j < embed_dim; j++) {
                    float d = (s_x[t * embed_dim + j] + s_t1[t * embed_dim + j]) - mean;
                    var += d * d;
                }
                var *= (1.0f / (float)embed_dim);
                float inv_std = rsqrtf(var + 1e-5f);
                const float* n2w = norm2_weight + layer * embed_dim;
                const float* n2b = norm2_bias + layer * embed_dim;
                for (int j = 0; j < embed_dim; j++) {
                    s_x[t * embed_dim + j] = ((s_x[t * embed_dim + j] + s_t1[t * embed_dim + j]) - mean) * inv_std * n2w[j] + n2b[j];
                }
            }
        }
        __syncthreads();
    }
    
    // FC out on CLS token (first token)
    const float* w_fcout = fc_out_weight;
    const float* b_fcout = fc_out_bias;
    float* out_g = output + b * num_classes;
    for (int od = tid; od < num_classes; od += blockDim.x) {
        float acc = b_fcout[od];
        for (int i = 0; i < embed_dim; i++) {
            acc += s_x[i] * w_fcout[i * num_classes + od];
        }
        out_g[od] = acc;
    }
}

void fused_transformer_launch(
    torch::Tensor x,
    torch::Tensor output,
    torch::Tensor norm1_weight,
    torch::Tensor norm1_bias,
    torch::Tensor qkv_weight,
    torch::Tensor qkv_bias,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_weight,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_bias,
    torch::Tensor norm2_weight,
    torch::Tensor norm2_bias,
    torch::Tensor fc1_weight,
    torch::Tensor fc1_bias,
    torch::Tensor fc2_weight,
    torch::Tensor fc2_bias,
    torch::Tensor fc_out_weight,
    torch::Tensor fc_out_bias,
    int num_layers,
    int num_heads
) {
    int B = x.size(0);
    int seq_len = x.size(1);
    int embed_dim = x.size(2);
    int mlp_dim = fc1_bias.size(1);
    int num_classes = output.size(1);
    
    int score_size = num_heads * seq_len * seq_len;
    int s_t2_size = (score_size > seq_len * mlp_dim) ? score_size : seq_len * mlp_dim;
    int shared_mem = (seq_len * embed_dim +
                      seq_len * embed_dim +
                      seq_len * 3 * embed_dim +
                      s_t2_size) * sizeof(float);
    
    const int threads = 128;
    fused_transformer_kernel<<<B, threads, shared_mem>>>(
        x.data_ptr<float>(),
        output.data_ptr<float>(),
        norm1_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        norm1_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        qkv_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        qkv_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        out_proj_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        out_proj_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        norm2_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        norm2_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        fc1_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        fc1_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        fc2_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        fc2_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        fc_out_weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        fc_out_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, num_layers, seq_len, embed_dim, num_heads, mlp_dim, num_classes
    );
}
"""

module = load_inline(
    name='fused_transformer_postln',
    cpp_sources=cpp_source,
    cuda_sources=cuda_code,
    functions=['fused_transformer_launch'],
    verbose=False
)

fused_transformer_launch = module.fused_transformer_launch

class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, num_classes, embed_dim=512, num_heads=8, num_layers=6, 
                 mlp_ratio=4.0, patch_size=4, in_channels=3, image_size=32):
        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()

        self.patch_size = patch_size
        self.image_size = image_size
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim

        self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, embed_dim, kernel_size=patch_size, stride=patch_size)
        num_patches = (image_size // patch_size) ** 2
        self.linear_proj = nn.Linear(embed_dim * num_patches, embed_dim)

        self.transformer_layers = nn.ModuleList([
            nn.TransformerEncoderLayer(
                d_model=embed_dim,
                nhead=num_heads,
                dim_feedforward=int(embed_dim * mlp_ratio),
                dropout=0.0,
                batch_first=True
            ) for _ in range(num_layers)
        ])

        self.cls_token = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, 1, embed_dim))
        self.fc_out = nn.Linear(embed_dim, num_classes)
        
    def forward(self, x):
        B = x.size(0)
        x = self.conv1(x)
        x = x.flatten(start_dim=1)
        x = self.linear_proj(x)

        cls_tokens = self.cls_token.expand(B, -1, -1)
        x = torch.cat((cls_tokens, x.unsqueeze(1)), dim=1).contiguous()
        
        # Extract transformer weights
        norm1_w = torch.stack([layer.norm1.weight for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        norm1_b = torch.stack([layer.norm1.bias for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        qkv_w = torch.stack([layer.self_attn.in_proj_weight.t().contiguous() for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        qkv_b = torch.stack([layer.self_attn.in_proj_bias for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        out_w = torch.stack([layer.self_attn.out_proj.weight.t().contiguous() for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        out_b = torch.stack([layer.self_attn.out_proj.bias for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        norm2_w = torch.stack([layer.norm2.weight for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        norm2_b = torch.stack([layer.norm2.bias for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        fc1_w = torch.stack([layer.linear1.weight.t().contiguous() for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        fc1_b = torch.stack([layer.linear1.bias for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        fc2_w = torch.stack([layer.linear2.weight.t().contiguous() for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        fc2_b = torch.stack([layer.linear2.bias for layer in self.transformer_layers])
        
        fc_out_w = self.fc_out.weight.t().contiguous()
        fc_out_b = self.fc_out.bias
        
        output = torch.empty(B, self.fc_out.out_features, device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
        
        fused_transformer_launch(
            x, output,
            norm1_w, norm1_b,
            qkv_w, qkv_b,
            out_w, out_b,
            norm2_w, norm2_b,
            fc1_w, fc1_b,
            fc2_w, fc2_b,
            fc_out_w, fc_out_b,
            len(self.transformer_layers), self.transformer_layers[0].self_attn.num_heads
        )
        return output
